The bathroom equipment that I am most concerned about is very easy to use. The faucet is easy to use and hot water comes out as soon as it is turned on. They enthusiastically introduced the various facilities of the hotel, and especially reminded that there is a self-service washing machine on the fifth floor that can be used for free. Although we didn't have time to use it, this should be a very friendly service content for tourists.
